3176 priority: 100,
3177 synchronization_address: 7962,

3180 stream_terminated: false,
3181 force_synchronization: false,
3182 universe: 1,
31832 data: DataPacketDmpLayer {
31842 property_values: TEST_DATA_PACKET_EMPTY[125..].into(),
3185 },
3186 }),
3187 },
3188 };
3189
31902 assert_eq!(
31912 AcnRootLayerProtocol::parse(&TEST_DATA_PACKET_EMPTY).unwrap(),
3192 packet
3193 );
3194

31962 packet.pack(&mut buf).unwrap();

31994}
